    5962                 : /* {{{ _reflection_write_property */
    5963               0 : static void _reflection_write_property(zval *object, zval *member, zval *value, const zend_literal *key TSRMLS_DC)
    5964                 : {
    5965               0 :         if ((Z_TYPE_P(member) == IS_STRING)
